***невозможно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a> (899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможный.html>невозмо́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevozmóžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevozmóžno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>impossibly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevozmóžno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>it is impossible</li>
<li>there is no way <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to do something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The predicative <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></b> is synonymous with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></b> with a perfective infinite verb. Thus, sentences with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></b> require perfective infinitives.
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>кака́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бочок.html>бо́чка</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>Её</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kakája tjažólaja bóčka! Jejó <b>nevozmóžno</b> podnjátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What a heavy barrel! It's impossible to lift it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>

***невозможный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невозможный.html>невозмо́жный</a> (4044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возможный.html>возмо́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozmóžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невольно.html>нево́льно</a> (2463)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́ля</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vólja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невольно.html>нево́льно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevólʹno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>involuntarily</li>
<li>automatically</li>
<li>unintentionally, unwittingly</li></ol>

<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невольный.html>нево́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevólʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>forced</li>
<li>involuntary, unintentional

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вредить.html>вреди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vredítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невредимый.html>невреди́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevredímyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)невреди́мее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)невреди́мей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>unscathed, unharmed, unhurt, safe, intact
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>цел</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:невредимый.html>невреди́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">cel i nevredim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">safe and sound</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***невропатолог.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невропатолог.html>невропато́лог</a> (19148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">невропатоло́гия</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevropatológija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невропатолог.html>невропато́лог</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevropatólog</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невропатолог.html>невропато́лога</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невропатолог.html>невропато́логи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невропатолог.html>невропато́логов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>neuropathologist</li>
<li>neurologist <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">former usage up till about 1980, incorrect, occasionally still found</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невыгодный.html>невы́годный</a> (18743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выгодный.html>вы́годный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výgodnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невыгодный.html>невы́годный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevýgodnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unprofitable, non-lucrative, unremunerative, not paying</li>
<li>disadvantageous, unfavourable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невыгодный.html>невы́годной</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pokazátʹ sebjá s <b>nevýgodnoj</b> storony</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show oneself to disadvantage; place oneself in an unfavourable light</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невыгодный.html>невы́годное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stávitʹ v <b>nevýgodnoje</b> položénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">place at a disadvantage; handicap</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:оказаться.html>оказа́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невыгодный.html>невы́годном</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́нии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ/okazátʹsja v <b>nevýgodnom</b> položénii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be at a disadvantage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>unattractive</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невыезд.html>невы́езд</a> (22576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезд.html>вы́езд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výjezd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невыезд.html>невы́езд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevýjezd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невыезд.html>невы́езда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невыезд.html>невы́езды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невыезд.html>невы́ездов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>period of not leaving a given city or country</li>
<li>prohibition on leaving a given city or country</li></ol>

***невыполнимый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невыполнимый.html>невыполни́мый</a> (21693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выполнимый.html>выполни́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vypolnímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невыразительный.html>невырази́тельный</a> (19083)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выразительный.html>вырази́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyrazítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невыразительный.html>невырази́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevyrazítelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)невырази́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)невырази́тельней</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невыясненный.html>невы́ясненный</a> (25659)</h1><br><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Холин впервые выделен в 1849 г. из фосфолипидов желчи и получен в чистом виде в 1862 г. Strecker. Однако химическая структура и биологическая роль холина долго оставались <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">невыясненными</span>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

<ol><li>there is no place to (negative of <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> stilted</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> somewhere
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">где́-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gdé-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
